<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/2013_French_Open" title="2013 French Open">2013 French Open</a></div>
<p><a href="/wiki/Annika_Beck" title="Annika Beck">Annika Beck</a> was the 2012 champion, but was no longer eligible to compete in junior tennis, and thus couldn't defend her title.
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Belinda_Bencic" title="Belinda Bencic">Belinda Bencic</a> won her first junior grand slam, defeating doubles partner <a href="/wiki/Antonia_Lottner" title="Antonia Lottner">Antonia Lottner</a> in the final, 6–1, 6–3.
</p>
